***перевозить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перевозить.html>перевози́ть</a> (11579)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возить.html>вози́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vozítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перевозить.html>перевози́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perevozítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перевезти.html>перевезти́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to transport, to carry (by vehicle), to remove, to move
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перевозить.html>перевози́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пассажир.html>пассажи́ров</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perevozítʹ</b> passažírov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to carry passengers</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перевозить.html>перевози́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:груз.html>груз</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:железный.html>желе́зной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́ге</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:водный.html>во́дным</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:путь.html>путём</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perevozítʹ</b> gruz po želéznoj doróge (vódnym putjóm)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to carry freight by rail (by water)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перевозить.html>перевози́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:корабль.html>корабле́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perevozítʹ</b> na korablé</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to ship</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перевозить.html>перевози́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:телега.html>теле́ге</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perevozítʹ</b> na telége</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to cart</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to take across, to put across</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">перево́з</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">perevóz</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перевозка.html>перево́зка</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">perevózka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">перево́зочный</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">perevózočnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перевозчик.html>перево́зчик</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">perevózčik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перевозить.html>перевози́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perevozítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">перева́живать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to transport, to carry (by vehicle) all, to transport, to carry too many
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>Не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:беспокоиться.html>беспоко́йся</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уже.html>уже́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:перевозить.html>перевози́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:столько.html>сто́лько</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кинозвезда.html>кинозвёзд</a>!</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ne bespokójsja, ja užé <b>perevozíl</b> stólʹko kinozvjózd!</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Don't worry, I have already driven so many movie stars!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***перевозка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перевозка.html>перево́зка</a> (8962)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перевозить.html>перевози́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perevozítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>

***перевоспитавший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перевоспитать.html>перевоспита́вший</a> (24649)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перевоспитать.html>перевоспита́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perevospitávšij</span>)

***перевязать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перевязать.html>перевяза́ть</a> (7605)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вязать.html>вяза́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vjazátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перевязать.html>перевяза́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perevjazátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перевязывать.html>перевя́зывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to tie up, to cord</li>
<li>to tie up again, to cord again</li>
<li>to bandage
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перевязать.html>перевяза́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рана.html>ра́ну</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perevjazátʹ</b> ránu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to dress the wound; change the dressing</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to knit again, to have knitted again
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перевязать.html>перевяза́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кофта.html>ко́фту</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perevjazátʹ</b> kóftu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">knit the jacket again; have the jacket knitted again</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перевязка.html>перевя́зка</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">perevjázka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перевязочный.html>перевя́зочный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">perevjázočnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перевязь.html>пе́ревязь</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pérevjazʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***перевязывавший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перевязывать.html>перевя́зывавший</a> (18136)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перевязывать.html>перевя́зывавший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perevjázyvavšij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перевязывать.html>перевя́зывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perevjázyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***перевязывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перевязывать.html>перевя́зывать</a> (18136)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перевязать.html>перевяза́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perevjazátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перевязывать.html>перевя́зывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perevjázyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перевязать.html>перевяза́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to tie up, to cord</li>
<li>to tie up again, to cord again</li>
<li>to bandage
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перевязывать.html>перевя́зывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рана.html>ра́ну</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perevjázyvatʹ</b> ránu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to dress the wound; change the dressing</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to knit again, to have knitted again</li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перевязка.html>перевя́зка</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">perevjázka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перевязочный.html>перевя́зочный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">perevjázočnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перевязь.html>пе́ревязь</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pérevjazʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***перегиб.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перегиб.html>переги́б</a> (28320)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перегибать.html>перегиба́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">peregibátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перегиб.html>переги́б</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peregíb</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перегиб.html>переги́ба</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перегиб.html>переги́бы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перегиб.html>переги́бов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>bend</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> excess, extreme</li></ol>

***перегибать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перегибать.html>перегиба́ть</a> (31787)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-гиба́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-gibátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перегибать.html>перегиба́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peregibátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перегнуть.html>перегну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fold, to bend</li>
<li>to go to extremes
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перегибать.html>перегиба́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:палка.html>па́лку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">peregibátʹ pálku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to go too far</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***перегнать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перегнать.html>перегна́ть</a> (18666)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гнать.html>гнать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gnatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перегнать.html>перегна́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peregnátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перегонять.html>перегоня́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to drive (somewhere else), to ferry</li>
<li>to distill</li>
<li>to surpass, to overtake</li>
<li>to outrun, to outdistance</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гнуть.html>гнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перегнуть.html>перегну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peregnútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перегибать.html>перегиба́ть</a></b>)

***перегнуться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перегнуться.html>перегну́ться</a> (11371)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перегнуть.html>перегну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">peregnútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перегнуться.html>перегну́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peregnútʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">перегиба́ться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to bend</li>
<li>to lean over, to lean <i>(over)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:перегнуться.html>перегну́лся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:через.html>че́рез</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:перила.html>пери́ла</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>peregnúlsja</b> čerez períla</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he leaned over the banisters/rail</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перегнуть.html>перегну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">peregnútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
